Emerging growth company <ix:nonNumeric contextRef="c-1" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" format="ixt:fixed-false" id="f-22">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric> </span></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt;margin-top:2pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#160;&#9744; </span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="height:42.75pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><span><br/></span></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span><br/></span></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span style="color:#5f0095;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:22pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Item&#160;2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On December&#160;19, 2023, Accenture plc (&#8220;Accenture&#8221;) issued a news release announcing financial results for its first quarter of fiscal 2024, which ended on November&#160;30, 2023.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A copy of the news release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99. All information in the news release is furnished but not filed.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:110%">Non-GAAP Financial Information</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the attached news release Accenture discloses the following non-GAAP financial measures:</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Free cash flow (defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions). Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Adjusted financial measures excluding the impact of business optimization costs and gain on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the business optimization costs and the investment gain facilitates an understanding as to the impact of these items and the company&#8217;s performance in comparison to the prior period.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:9pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span style="color:#5f0095;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:22pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Item&#160;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">(d)&#160;Exhibits</span></div><div continues to expect revenue growth of 2% to 5% in local currency&#59; GAAP EPS of $11.41 to $11.76, a 6% to 9% increase&#59; and adjusted EPS of $11.97 to $12.32, a 3% to 6% increase</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; December&#160;19, 2023 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the first quarter of fiscal 2024 ended November&#160;30, 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Julie Sweet, chair and CEO, Accenture, said, &#8220;I am pleased that we delivered on our commitments this quarter while strategically investing at scale for future growth. Our deep and trusted client relationships are again reflected in the 30 clients with quarterly bookings of more than $100 million. And we continue to lead our industry in Gen AI &#8211; the great accelerator of reinvention &#8211; with over $450 million in new bookings. I am incredibly grateful to the </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">743,000</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> people of Accenture, who are steadfastly dedicated to helping our clients achieve their ambition to grow and thrive in the years ahead.&#8221; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues were $16.2 billion, an increase of 3% in U.S. dollars and 1% in local currency over the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP operating income was $2.56 billion, compared to $2.59 billion for the first quarter of fiscal 2023, and operating margin was 15.8% compared to 16.5% for the first quarter last year. Adjusted operating income was $2.70 billion and adjusted operating margin was 16.7%, an expansion of 20 basis points from the first quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted earnings per share were $3.10, compared to $3.08 for the first quarter of fiscal 2023. Adjusted EPS were $3.27, an increase of 6% from the first quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the quarter were $18.4 billion, with consulting bookings of $8.6 billion and managed services bookings of $9.8 billion.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted financial measures presented in this release are non-GAAP financial measures that exclude business optimization costs, as further described in this release.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><br></font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the first quarter of fiscal 2024 were $16.22 billion, compared with $15.75 billion for the first quarter of fiscal 2023, an increase of 3% in U.S. dollars and 1% in local currency. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the quarter reflect a foreign-exchange impact of approximately positive 1.5% compared with the positive 2.5% impact previously assumed. Adjusting for the actual foreign-exchange impact, the company&#8217;s guided range for quarterly revenues was approximately $15.70 billion to $16.30 billion. Accenture&#8217;s first quarter fiscal 2024 revenues were at the top end of this adjusted range.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Consulting revenues for the quarter were $8.46 billion, flat in U.S. dollars and a decrease of 2% in local currency compared with the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Managed Services revenues for the quarter were $7.77 billion, an increase of 6% in U.S. dollars and 5% in local currency compared with the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted EPS for the quarter were $3.10 compared with $3.08 for the first quarter of fiscal 2023. Excluding a $0.17 decrease for business optimization costs, adjusted EPS were $3.27, an increase of 6% from the first quarter of fiscal 2023. The $0.19 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.14&#160;increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.05 increase from higher non-operating income&#59; and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01 increase from lower share count&#59; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">      partially offset by</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01&#160;decrease from higher noncontrolling interests.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the quarter was 33.6% compared to 32.9% in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. Selling, general and administrative (SG&#38;A) expenses for the quarter were $2.74 billion, or 16.9% of revenues, compared with $2.59 billion, or 16.5% of revenues, for the first quarter of fiscal 2023.     </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP operating income for the quarter decreased 1%, to $2.56 billion, or 15.8% of revenues, compared with $2.59 billion, or 16.5% of revenues, for the first quarter of fiscal 2023. Adjusted operating income for the quarter was $2.70 billion, or 16.7% of revenues, an expansion of 20 basis points from the first quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company&#8217;s GAAP effective tax rate for the quarter was 23.2%, compared with 23.3% for the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP net income for the quarter was $2.01 billion, compared with $2.00 billion for the first quarter of fiscal 2023. Adjusted net income for the quarter was $2.12 billion.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating cash flow for the quarter was $499 million, and property and equipment additions were $69 million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $430 million. For the same period last year, operating cash flow was $495 million&#59; property and equipment additions were $99 million&#59; and free cash flow was $397 million.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 49 days at November&#160;30, 2023, compared with 42 days at August&#160;31, 2023 and 48 days at November&#160;30, 2022. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s total cash balance at November&#160;30, 2023 was $7.1 billion, compared with $9.0 billion at August&#160;31, 2023.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">New Bookings</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the first quarter of fiscal 2024 were $18.45 billion, a 14% increase in U.S. dollars and a 12% increase in local currency over the first quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Consulting new bookings were $8.62 billion, or 47% of total new bookings.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font
